async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const { user_type, raw_transcript, page_route } = req.body;\n        console.log(`[${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}] ${user_type}: \"${raw_transcript}\"`);\n        \n        const lower = (raw_transcript || '').toLowerCase();\n        const sentiment = lower.includes('?') ? 'curiosity' : (lower.match(/good|great|thank|love/) ? 'positive' : (lower.match(/bad|hate|angry|frustrat/) ? 'negative' : 'neutral'));\n        const intent = lower.match(/show|open|go|navigate/) ? 'navigation' : (lower.match(/help|how|what/) ? 'query' : 'general');\n        const empathyScore = sentiment === 'positive' ? 0.85 : (sentiment === 'negative' ? 0.45 : 0.7);\n        \n        // Insert ledger\n        const ledger = await pool.query(\n            `INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger (user_type, raw_transcript, page_route, sentiment, emotion, intent, empathy_score, created_at)\n             VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, NOW()) RETURNING id`,\n            [user_type, raw_transcript, page_route || '/dashboard', sentiment, sentiment, intent, empathyScore]\n        );\n        \n        // Boss input\n        if (user_type === 'boss') {\n            await pool.query(`INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_text, processed, priority, created_at) VALUES ($1, false, 'high', NOW())`, [raw_transcript]);\n        }\n        \n        // Feed\n        await pool.query(\n            `INSERT INTO realtime_feed (feed_type, title, description, user_type, icon, page_context, created_at)\n             VALUES ('voice', $1, $2, $3, '\ud83c\udfa4', $4, NOW())`,\n            [`${user_type}: \"${raw_transcript.substring(0,30)}...\"`, `${intent} | ${sentiment}`, user_type, page_route || '/']\n        );\n        \n        // Learn pattern\n        await pool.query(\n            `INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_name, pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, created_at) \n             VALUES ($1, $2, $3, 1, NOW())`,\n            [raw_transcript.substring(0,50), raw_transcript, intent]\n        );\n        \n        // Update stats\n        await pool.query(`\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET\n                total_interactions = COALESCE(total_interactions,0) + 1,\n                ledger_entries = COALESCE(ledger_entries,0) + 1,\n                boss_inputs = COALESCE(boss_inputs,0) + $1,\n                patterns_learned = COALESCE(patterns_learned,0) + 1,\n                tts_responses_given = COALESCE(tts_responses_given,0) + 1,\n                updated_at = NOW()\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\n        `, [user_type === 'boss' ? 1 : 0]);\n        \n        // Generate empathetic response\n        let ttsText = \"I understand. How can I help you?\";\n        if (sentiment === 'positive') ttsText = \"That's wonderful! I'm happy to help.\";\n        else if (sentiment === 'negative') ttsText = \"I understand your concern. Let me help resolve this.\";\n        else if (intent === 'navigation') ttsText = \"I'll take you there right away.\";\n        else if (intent === 'query') ttsText = \"Great question! Let me find that for you.\";\n        if (user_type === 'boss') ttsText = \"Got it, boss! I'm on it right away.\";\n        \n        res.json({\n            success: true,\n            ledger_id: ledger.rows[0].id,\n            analysis: { sentiment, emotion: sentiment, intent, empathyScore },\n            tts_response: { text: ttsText, tone: 'friendly' }\n        });\n    } catch (err) {\n        console.error('[ERROR]', err.message);\n        res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });\n    }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n//           headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({\n                user_type: userType,\n                raw_transcript: text,\n                page_route: \"\"\necho \"\ud83c\udfa4 STEP 5: Creating FIXED useVoice hook...\"\n\ncat > \"$VV/frontend/src/hooks/useVoice.ts\" << 'VOICEHOOK'\n/**\n * VISTAVIEW VOICE HOOK - FIXED VERSION\n * Handles speech recognition and synthesis properly\n */\n\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\nimport { sendToAgentic } from '../utils/agenticAPI';\n\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\n    onTranscript?: (text: string, isFinal: boolean) => void;\n    onResponse?: (response: any) => void;\n    onStateChange?: (state: VoiceState) => void;\n    userType?: string;\n    continuous?: boolean;\n}\n\ntype VoiceState = 'idle' | 'listening' | 'processing' | 'speaking' | 'error';\n\nexport function useVoice(options: UseVoiceOptions = {}) {\n    const [state, setState] = useState<VoiceState>('idle');\n    const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n    const [isSupported, setIsSupported] = useState(false);\n    \n    const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\n    const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\n    const isListeningRef = useRef(false);\n    const shouldRestartRef = useRef(false);\n    \n    // Initialize\n    useEffect(() => {\n        // Check browser support\n        const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n        \n        if (!SpeechRecognition) {\n            console.warn('[useVoice] Speech recognition not supported');\n            setError('Speech recognition not supported in this browser');\n            setIsSupported(false);\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        setIsSupported(true);\n        synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\n        \n        // Create recognition instance\n        const recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\n        recognition.continuous = options.continuous ?? true;\n        recognition.interimResults = true;\n        recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n        recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;\n        \n        recognition.onstart = () => {\n            console.log('[useVoice] \u2705 Started listening');\n            isListeningRef.current = true;\n            setState('listening');\n            options.onStateChange?.('listening');\n        };\n        \n        recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {\n            let interimTranscript = '';\n            let finalTranscript = '';\n            \n            for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n                const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript;\n                if (event.results[i].isFinal) {\n                    finalTranscript += transcript;\n                } else {\n                    interimTranscript += transcript;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            const currentText = finalTranscript || interimTranscript;\n            setTranscript(currentText);\n            options.onTranscript?.(currentText, !!finalTranscript);\n            \n            // If we got final transcript, process it\n            if (finalTranscript && finalTranscript.trim()) {\n                processInput(finalTranscript.trim());\n            }\n        };\n        \n        recognition.onerror = (event: any) => {\n            console.error('[useVoice] Error:', event.error);\n            \n            // Don't treat \"aborted\" or \"no-speech\" as real errors\n            if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') {\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n                setError('Microphone access denied. Please allow microphone access.');\n                setState('error');\n            }\n        };\n        \n        recognition.onend = () => {\n            console.log('[useVoice] Recognition ended');\n            isListeningRef.current = false;\n            \n            // Restart if we should be listening\n            if (shouldRestartRef.current && state !== 'speaking') {\n                setTimeout(() => {\n                    if (shouldRestartRef.current) {\n                        try {\n                            recognition.start();\n                        } catch (e) {\n                            // Already started, ignore\n                        }\n                    }\n                }, 100);\n            } else {\n                setState('idle');\n            }\n        };\n        \n        recognitionRef.current = recognition;\n        \n        return () => {\n            shouldRestartRef.current = false;\n            recognition.stop();\n        };\n    }, []);\n    \n    // Process input and send to backend\n    const processInput = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\n        setState('processing');\n        options.onStateChange?.('processing');\n        \n        try {\n            const response = await sendToAgentic(text, options.userType || 'visitor');\n            options.onResponse?.(response);\n            \n            // Speak response\n            if (response?.tts_response?.text && synthRef.current) {\n                speak(response.tts_response.text);\n            } else {\n                setState('idle');\n            }\n        } catch (e) {\n            console.error('[useVoice] Process error:', e);\n            setState('idle');\n        }\n    }, [options.userType]);\n    \n    // Start listening\n    const startListening = useCallback(() => {\n        if (!recognitionRef.current) {\n            console.error('[useVoice] Recognition not initialized');\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        // Stop any speech first\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\n        \n        shouldRestartRef.current = true;\n        \n        if (!isListeningRef.current) {\n            try {\n                recognitionRef.current.start();\n            } catch (e) {\n                // Already started\n            }\n        }\n    }, []);\n    \n    // Stop listening\n    const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\n        shouldRestartRef.current = false;\n        \n        if (recognitionRef.current && isListeningRef.current) {\n            recognitionRef.current.stop();\n        }\n        \n        setState('idle');\n        options.onStateChange?.('idle');\n    }, []);\n    \n    // Toggle listening\n    const toggleListening = useCallback(() => {\n        if (isListeningRef.current || state === 'listening') {\n            stopListening();\n        } else {\n            startListening();\n        }\n    }, [state, startListening, stopListening]);\n    \n    // Speak text\n    const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n        if (!synthRef.current) return;\n        \n        // Stop listening while speaking\n        const wasListening = isListeningRef.current;\n        if (wasListening) {\n            shouldRestartRef.current = false;\n            recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n        }\n        \n        synthRef.current.cancel();\n        \n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n        utterance.rate = 0.95;\n        utterance.pitch = 1;\n        utterance.volume = 1;\n        \n        utterance.onstart = () => {\n            setState('speaking');\n            options.onStateChange?.('speaking');\n        };\n        \n        utterance.onend = () => {\n            setState('idle');\n            options.onStateChange?.('idle');\n            \n            // Restart listening if we were listening before\n            if (wasListening && options.continuous) {\n                setTimeout(startListening, 200);\n            }\n        };\n        \n        synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\n    }, [options.continuous, startListening]);\n    \n    // Stop speaking\n    const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\n        setState('idle');\n    }, []);\n    \n    return {\n        state,\n        transcript,\n        error,\n        isSupported,\n        isListening: state === 'listening',\n        isSpeaking: state === 'speaking',\n        startListening,\n        stopListening,\n        toggleListening,\n        speak,\n        stopSpeaking,\n        processInput\n    };\n}\n\nexport default \\\"${raw_transcript}\\\"`);\\n        \\n        const lower = (raw_transcript || '').toLowerCase();\\n        const sentiment = lower.includes('?') ? Let me help resolve this.\\\";\\n        else if (intent === 'navigation') ttsText = \\\"I'll take you there right away.\\\";\\n        else if (intent === 'query') ttsText = \\\"Great question! \\\"$VV/frontend/src/utils/agenticAPI.ts\\\" << 'APIEOF'\\n/**\\n * VISTAVIEW AGENTIC API\\n * Connects frontend to backend (port 1117)\\n */\\n\\nconst AGENTIC_API =        user_type: userType,\\n                raw_transcript: text,\\n                page_route: pageRoute || window.location.pathname\\n            })\\n        });\\n        return STEP 5: Create FIXED useVoice.ts hook\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83c\\udfa4 STEP 5: Creating FIXED useVoice hook...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV/frontend/src/hooks/useVoice.ts\\\" << 'VOICEHOOK'\\n/**\\n * VISTAVIEW VOICE HOOK - FIXED VERSION\\n * Handles speech recognition and synthesis properly\\n */\\n\\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\\nimport { sendToAgentic } from '../utils/agenticAPI';\\n\\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\\n    onTranscript?: (text: string, isFinal: boolean) => void;\\n    onResponse?: (response: any) => void;\\n    onStateChange?: (state: VoiceState) => void;\\n    userType?: string;\\n    continuous?: boolean;\\n}\\n\\ntype VoiceState = 'idle' | 'listening' | 'processing' | 'speaking' | 'error';\\n\\nexport function useVoice(options: UseVoiceOptions = {}) {\\n    const [state, setState] = useState<VoiceState>('idle');\\n    const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\\n    const [isSupported, setIsSupported] = useState(false);\\n    \\n    const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\\n    const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n    const isListeningRef = useRef(false);\\n    const shouldRestartRef = useRef(false);\\n    \\n    // Initialize\\n    useEffect(() => {\\n        // Check browser support\\n        const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n        \\n        if (!SpeechRecognition) {\\n            console.warn('[useVoice] Speech recognition not supported');\\n            setError('Speech recognition not supported in this browser');\\n            setIsSupported(false);\\n            return;\\n        }\\n        \\n        setIsSupported(true);\\n        synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\\n        \\n        // Create recognition instance\\n        const recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\\n        recognition.continuous = options.continuous ?? true;\\n        recognition.interimResults = true;\\n        recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n        recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;\\n        \\n        recognition.onstart = () => {\\n            console.log('[useVoice] \\u2705 Started listening');\\n            isListeningRef.current = true;\\n            setState('listening');\\n            options.onStateChange?.('listening');\\n        };\\n        \\n        recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {\\n            let interimTranscript = '';\\n            let finalTranscript = '';\\n            \\n            for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n                const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n                if (event.results[i].isFinal) {\\n                    finalTranscript += transcript;\\n                } else {\\n                    interimTranscript += transcript;\\n                }\\n            }\\n            \\n            const currentText = finalTranscript || interimTranscript;\\n            setTranscript(currentText);\\n            options.onTranscript?.(currentText, !!finalTranscript);\\n            \\n            // If we got final transcript, process it\\n            if (finalTranscript && finalTranscript.trim()) {\\n                processInput(finalTranscript.trim());\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        recognition.onerror = (event: any) => {\\n            console.error('[useVoice] Error:', event.error);\\n            \\n            // Don't treat \\\"aborted\\\" or \\\"no-speech\\\" as real errors\\n            if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') {\\n                return;\\n            }\\n            \\n            if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n                setError('Microphone access denied. Please allow microphone access.');\\n                setState('error');\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        recognition.onend = () => {\\n            console.log('[useVoice] Recognition ended');\\n            isListeningRef.current = false;\\n            \\n            // Restart if we should be listening\\n            if (shouldRestartRef.current && state !== 'speaking') {\\n                setTimeout(() => {\\n                    if (shouldRestartRef.current) {\\n                        try {\\n                            recognition.start();\\n                        } catch (e) {\\n                            // Already started, ignore\\n                        }\\n                    }\\n                }, 100);\\n            } else {\\n                setState('idle');\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        recognitionRef.current = recognition;\\n        \\n        return () => {\\n            shouldRestartRef.current = false;\\n            recognition.stop();\\n        };\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    // Process input and send to backend\\n    const processInput = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\\n        setState('processing');\\n        options.onStateChange?.('processing');\\n        \\n        try {\\n            const response = await sendToAgentic(text, options.userType || 'visitor');\\n            options.onResponse?.(response);\\n            \\n            // Speak response\\n            if (response?.tts_response?.text && synthRef.current) {\\n                speak(response.tts_response.text);\\n            } else {\\n                setState('idle');\\n            }\\n        } catch (e) {\\n            console.error('[useVoice] Process error:', e);\\n            setState('idle');\\n        }\\n    }, [options.userType]);\\n    \\n    // Start listening\\n    const startListening = useCallback(() => {\\n        if (!recognitionRef.current) {\\n            console.error('[useVoice] Recognition not initialized');\\n            return;\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Stop any speech first\\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n        \\n        shouldRestartRef.current = true;\\n        \\n        if (!isListeningRef.current) {\\n            try {\\n                recognitionRef.current.start();\\n            } catch (e) {\\n                // Already started\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    // Stop listening\\n    const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\\n        shouldRestartRef.current = false;\\n        \\n        if (recognitionRef.current && isListeningRef.current) {\\n            recognitionRef.current.stop();\\n        }\\n        \\n        setState('idle');\\n        options.onStateChange?.('idle');\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    // Toggle listening\\n    const toggleListening = useCallback(() => {\\n        if (isListeningRef.current || state === 'listening') {\\n            stopListening();\\n        } else {\\n            startListening();\\n        }\\n    }, [state, startListening, stopListening]);\\n    \\n    // Speak text\\n    const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n        if (!synthRef.current) return;\\n        \\n        // Stop listening while speaking\\n        const wasListening = isListeningRef.current;\\n        if (wasListening) {\\n            shouldRestartRef.current = false;\\n            recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n        }\\n        \\n        synthRef.current.cancel();\\n        \\n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n        utterance.rate = 0.95;\\n        utterance.pitch = 1;\\n        utterance.volume = 1;\\n        \\n        utterance.onstart = () => {\\n            setState('speaking');\\n            options.onStateChange?.('speaking');\\n        };\\n        \\n        utterance.onend = () => {\\n            setState('idle');\\n            options.onStateChange?.('idle');\\n            \\n            // Restart listening if we were listening before\\n            if (wasListening && options.continuous) {\\n                setTimeout(startListening, 200);\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n    }, [options.continuous, startListening]);\\n    \\n    // Stop speaking\\n    const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n        setState('idle');\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    return {\\n        state,\\n        transcript,\\n        error,\\n        isSupported,\\n        isListening: state === 'listening',\\n        isSpeaking: state === 'speaking',\\n        startListening,\\n        stopListening,\\n        toggleListening,\\n        speak,\\n        stopSpeaking,\\n        processInput\\n    };\\n}\\n\\nexport default useVoice;\\nVOICEHOOK\\n\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# STEP 6: Restart everything\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho i++) {\n                const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript;\n                if (event.results[i].isFinal) {\n                    final += transcript;\n                } else {\n                    interim += transcript;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            const text = final || interim;\n            const isFinal = !!final;\n            \n            if (text !== this.lastTranscript) {\n                this.lastTranscript = text;\n                this.notifyListeners('onTranscript', text, isFinal);\n            }\n            \n            if (isFinal && final.trim()) {\n                this.processTranscript(final.trim());\n            }\n        };\n        \n        this.recognition.onerror = (event: any) => {\n            // Ignore harmless errors\n            if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') {\n                console.log('[VoiceManager] Harmless error:', event.error);\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            console.error('[VoiceManager] Error:', event.error);\n            \n            if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n                this.notifyListeners('onError', 'Microphone access denied');\n                this.setState('error');\n                this.shouldBeListening = false;\n            }\n        };\n        \n        this.recognition.onend = () => {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] Recognition ENDED, shouldBeListening:', this.shouldBeListening);\n            \n            // Clear any pending restart\n            if (this.restartTimeout) {\n                clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\n                this.restartTimeout = null;\n            }\n            \n            // Only restart if we should be listening AND not speaking\n            if (this.shouldBeListening && this.state !== 'speaking' && this.state !== 'paused') {\n                this.restartTimeout = setTimeout(() => {\n                    if (this.shouldBeListening && this.state !== 'speaking') {\n                        console.log('[VoiceManager] Restarting recognition...');\n                        this.startRecognition();\n                    }\n                }, 300); // Small delay to prevent rapid restart loop\n            } else {\n                this.setState('idle');\n            }\n        };\n        \n        this.isInitialized = true;\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] \u2705 Initialized');\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Subscribe to voice events\n     */\n    subscribe(listener: VoiceListener): () => void {\n        this.listeners.add(listener);\n        // Immediately notify of current state\n        listener.onStateChange?.(this.state);\n        \n        return () => {\n            this.listeners.delete(listener);\n        };\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Start listening\n     */\n    start(): void {\n        if (!this.isInitialized) {\n            this.init();\n        }\n        \n        console.log('[VoiceManager] START requested, current state:', this.state);\n        \n        // Stop any TTS first\n        this.stopSpeaking();\n        \n        this.shouldBeListening = true;\n        \n        if (this.state !== 'listening') {\n            this.startRecognition();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Stop listening\n     */\n    stop(): void {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] STOP requested');\n        \n        this.shouldBeListening = false;\n        \n        if (this.restartTimeout) {\n            clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\n            this.restartTimeout = null;\n        }\n        \n        try {\n            this.recognition?.stop();\n        } catch (e) {\n            // Ignore\n        }\n        \n        this.setState('idle');\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Toggle listening\n     */\n    toggle(): void {\n        if (this.shouldBeListening || this.state === 'listening') {\n            this.stop();\n        } else {\n            this.start();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Pause listening (for TTS)\n     */\n    pause(): void {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] PAUSE');\n        \n        if (this.restartTimeout) {\n            clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\n            this.restartTimeout = null;\n        }\n        \n        try {\n            this.recognition?.stop();\n        } catch (e) {}\n        \n        this.setState('paused');\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Resume listening (after TTS)\n     */\n    resume(): void {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] RESUME, shouldBeListening:', this.shouldBeListening);\n        \n        if (this.shouldBeListening) {\n            setTimeout(() => {\n                if (this.shouldBeListening && this.state !== 'speaking') {\n                    this.startRecognition();\n                }\n            }, 200);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Speak text (TTS) - automatically pauses STT\n     */\n    speak(text: string): void {\n        if (!this.synthesis) return;\n        \n        console.log('[VoiceManager] SPEAK:', text.substring(0, 50) + '...');\n        \n        // DUPLEX POLICY: Stop listening while speaking\n        this.pause();\n        \n        // Cancel any current speech\n        this.synthesis.cancel();\n        \n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n        utterance.rate = 0.95;\n        utterance.pitch = 1;\n        utterance.volume = 1;\n        \n        utterance.onstart = () => {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] TTS started');\n            this.setState('speaking');\n        };\n        \n        utterance.onend = () => {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] TTS ended');\n            this.currentUtterance = null;\n            \n            // DUPLEX POLICY: Resume listening after speaking\n            this.resume();\n        };\n        \n        utterance.onerror = (e) => {\n            console.error('[VoiceManager] TTS error:', e);\n            this.currentUtterance = null;\n            this.resume();\n        };\n        \n        this.currentUtterance = utterance;\n        this.synthesis.speak(utterance);\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Stop speaking\n     */\n    stopSpeaking(): void {\n        if (this.synthesis) {\n            this.synthesis.cancel();\n        }\n        this.currentUtterance = null;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Set mode\n     */\n    setMode(mode: VoiceMode): void {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] Mode:', mode);\n        this.mode = mode;\n        \n        if (mode === 'text') {\n            this.stop();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Get current state\n     */\n    getState(): VoiceState {\n        return this.state;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Get current mode\n     */\n    getMode(): VoiceMode {\n        return this.mode;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Check if listening\n     */\n    isListening(): boolean {\n        return this.state === 'listening';\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Check if speaking\n     */\n    isSpeaking(): boolean {\n        return this.state === 'speaking';\n    }\n    \n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n (!e.message?.includes('already started')) {\n                console.error('[VoiceManager] Start error:', e);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    private setState(newState: VoiceState): void this.notifyListeners('onStateChange', newState);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    private notifyListeners(event: keyof VoiceListener, ...args: any[]): void {\n        this.listeners.forEach(listener => {\n            const handler = listener[event];\n            if (typeof handler === 'function') {\n                (handler as Function)(...args);\n            }\n        });\n    }\n    \n    private async processTranscript(text: string): Promise<void> {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] Processing:', text);\n        this.setState('processing');\n        \n        try {\n            // Send to backend\n            const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/ledger/log', {\n                method: 'POST',\n                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({\n                    user_type: 'boss',\n                    raw_transcript: text,\n                    page_route: window.location.pathname\n                })\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            this.notifyListeners('onResponse', data);\n            \n            // Speak response if in talkative mode\n \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udcdd Creating integration instructions...\"\n\ncat > \"$VV/frontend/VOICE_FIX_INSTRUCTIONS.md\" << 'MDEOF'\n# \ud83e\udde0 VOICE FIX INSTRUCTIONS\n\n## THE PROBLEM\nTwo voice systems (VoiceBrain + useVoice) were fighting for the microphone.\nBrowser aborts when multiple recognition instances compete \u2192 infinite loop.\n\n## THE SOLUTION\nSingle VoiceManager singleton that OWNS the microphone.\nAll components subscribe to it instead of creating their own recognition.\n\n## FILES CREATED\n\n1. `src/lib/VoiceManager.ts` - The singleton (ONE mic owner)\n2. `src/hooks/useVoiceManager.ts` - React hook to use VoiceManager\n3. `src/components/AgenticBar.tsx` - Unified voice control bar\n\n## HOW TO INTEGRATE\n\n### Step 1: Update MrVAssistant.tsx\n\nRemove these imports:\n```typescript\n// REMOVE:\nimport { useVoice } from '../hooks/useVoice';\nimport VoiceBrain from './VoiceBrain';\n```\n\nAdd this import:\n```typescript\n// ADD:\nimport { useVoiceManager } from '../hooks/useVoiceManager';\n```\n\nReplace voice hook usage:\n```typescript\n// BEFORE:\nconst { isListening, transcript, ... } = useVoice();\n\n// AFTER:\nconst { isListening, transcript, state, toggle, speak } = useVoiceManager();\n```\n\n### Step 2: Remove VoiceBrain component\n\nIf you have `<VoiceBrain />` anywhere, REMOVE IT.\nThe VoiceManager handles everything now.\n\n### Step 3: Use AgenticBar globally\n\nIn your App.tsx or layout:\n```typescript\nimport { AgenticBar } from './components/AgenticBar';\n\nfunction App() {\n    return (\n        <>\n            {/* Your app content */}\n            <AgenticBar context=\"Home\" />\n        </>\n    );\n}\n```\n\n### Step 4: Initialize VoiceManager early\n\nIn your main entry (main.tsx or App.tsx):\n```typescript\nimport { voiceManager } from './lib/VoiceManager';\n\n// Initialize on app start\nvoiceManager.init();\n```\n\n## DUPLEX POLICY (IMPORTANT!)\n\nThe VoiceManager enforces:\n- When TTS starts \u2192 STT pauses automatically\n- When TTS ends \u2192 STT resumes automatically\n\nYou don't need to manage this manually.\n\n## TESTING\n\n1. Open console, should see:\n   - `[VoiceManager] \u2705 Initialized` (once)\n   - `[VoiceManager] \ud83c\udfa4 Recognition STARTED` (when you click mic)\n   - NO more `[VoiceBrain]` or duplicate `[VOICE]` logs\n\n2. Speak something:\n   - Should see `[VoiceManager] Processing: <your text>`\n   - Response from backend\n   - TTS plays (if talkative mode)\n   - STT resumes after TTS\n\n## TROUBLESHOOTING\n\nIf mic still loops:\n- Check there's NO other SpeechRecognition.start() anywhere\n- Search codebase for `webkitSpeechRecognition` - should only be in VoiceManager.ts\n- Check DevTools Network tab - should
